  <script type="text/javascript">
   //&lt;![CDATA[

/**
 * jQuery Mobile Menu 
 * Turn unordered list menu into dropdown select menu
 * version 1.0(31-OCT-2011)
 * 
 * Built on top of the jQuery library
 *   http://jquery.com
 * 
 * Documentation
 * 	 http://github.com/mambows/mobilemenu
 */
(function($){
$.fn.mobileMenu = function(options) {
	
	var defaults = {
			defaultText: 'Navigate to...',
			className: 'select-menu',
			containerClass: 'select-menu-container',
			subMenuClass: 'sub-menu',
			subMenuDash: '&ndash;'
		},
		settings = $.extend( defaults, options ),
		el = $(this);
	
	this.each(function(){
		// ad class to submenu list
		el.find('ul').addClass(settings.subMenuClass);

        // Create base menu
		$('&lt;div /&gt;',{
			'class' : settings.containerClass
		}).insertAfter( el );
        
		// Create base menu
		$('&lt;select /&gt;',{
			'class' : settings.className
		}).appendTo( '.' + settings.containerClass );

		// Create default option
		$('&lt;option /&gt;', {
			"value"		: '#',
			"text"		: settings.defaultText
		}).appendTo( '.' + settings.className );

		// Create select option from menu
		el.find('a').each(function(){
			var $this 	= $(this),
					optText	= '&nbsp;' + $this.text(),
					optSub	= $this.parents( '.' + settings.subMenuClass ),
					len			= optSub.length,
					dash;
			
			// if menu has sub menu
			if( $this.parents('ul').hasClass( settings.subMenuClass ) ) {
				dash = Array( len+1 ).join( settings.subMenuDash );
				optText = dash + optText;
			}

			// Now build menu and append it
			$('&lt;option /&gt;', {
				"value"	: this.href,
				"html"	: optText,
				"selected" : (this.href == window.location.href)
			}).appendTo( '.' + settings.className );

		}); // End el.find('a').each

		// Change event on select element
		$('.' + settings.className).change(function(){
			var locations = $(this).val();
			if( locations !== '#' ) {
				window.location.href = $(this).val();
			};
		});

	}); // End this.each

	return this;

};
})(jQuery);

//]]&gt;
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   //&lt;![CDATA[

(function($){
	/* hoverIntent by Brian Cherne */
	$.fn.hoverIntent = function(f,g) {
		// default configuration options
		var cfg = {
			sensitivity: 7,
			interval: 100,
			timeout: 0
		};
		// override configuration options with user supplied object
		cfg = $.extend(cfg, g ? { over: f, out: g } : f );

		// instantiate variables
		// cX, cY = current X and Y position of mouse, updated by mousemove event
		// pX, pY = previous X and Y position of mouse, set by mouseover and polling interval
		var cX, cY, pX, pY;

		// A private function for getting mouse position
		var track = function(ev) {
			cX = ev.pageX;
			cY = ev.pageY;
		};

		// A private function for comparing current and previous mouse position
		var compare = function(ev,ob) {
			ob.hoverIntent_t = clearTimeout(ob.hoverIntent_t);
			// compare mouse positions to see if they've crossed the threshold
			if ( ( Math.abs(pX-cX) + Math.abs(pY-cY) ) &lt; cfg.sensitivity ) {
				$(ob).unbind("mousemove",track);
				// set hoverIntent state to true (so mouseOut can be called)
				ob.hoverIntent_s = 1;
				return cfg.over.apply(ob,[ev]);
			} else {
				// set previous coordinates for next time
				pX = cX; pY = cY;
				// use self-calling timeout, guarantees intervals are spaced out properly (avoids JavaScript timer bugs)
				ob.hoverIntent_t = setTimeout( function(){compare(ev, ob);} , cfg.interval );
			}
		};

		// A private function for delaying the mouseOut function
		var delay = function(ev,ob) {
			ob.hoverIntent_t = clearTimeout(ob.hoverIntent_t);
			ob.hoverIntent_s = 0;
			return cfg.out.apply(ob,[ev]);
		};

		// A private function for handling mouse 'hovering'
		var handleHover = function(e) {
			// next three lines copied from jQuery.hover, ignore children onMouseOver/onMouseOut
			var p = (e.type == "mouseover" ? e.fromElement : e.toElement) || e.relatedTarget;
			while ( p &amp;&amp; p != this ) { try { p = p.parentNode; } catch(e) { p = this; } }
			if ( p == this ) { return false; }

			// copy objects to be passed into t (required for event object to be passed in IE)
			var ev = jQuery.extend({},e);
			var ob = this;

			// cancel hoverIntent timer if it exists
			if (ob.hoverIntent_t) { ob.hoverIntent_t = clearTimeout(ob.hoverIntent_t); }

			// else e.type == "onmouseover"
			if (e.type == "mouseover") {
				// set "previous" X and Y position based on initial entry point
				pX = ev.pageX; pY = ev.pageY;
				// update "current" X and Y position based on mousemove
				$(ob).bind("mousemove",track);
				// start polling interval (self-calling timeout) to compare mouse coordinates over time
				if (ob.hoverIntent_s != 1) { ob.hoverIntent_t = setTimeout( function(){compare(ev,ob);} , cfg.interval );}

			// else e.type == "onmouseout"
			} else {
				// unbind expensive mousemove event
				$(ob).unbind("mousemove",track);
				// if hoverIntent state is true, then call the mouseOut function after the specified delay
				if (ob.hoverIntent_s == 1) { ob.hoverIntent_t = setTimeout( function(){delay(ev,ob);} , cfg.timeout );}
			}
		};

		// bind the function to the two event listeners
		return this.mouseover(handleHover).mouseout(handleHover);
	};
	
})(jQuery);

//]]&gt;
  </script>

/*
 * Superfish v1.4.8 - jQuery menu widget
 * Copyright (c) 2008 Joel Birch
 *
 * Dual licensed under the MIT and GPL licenses:
 * 	http://www.opensource.org/licenses/mit-license.php
 * 	http://www.gnu.org/licenses/gpl.html
 *
 * CHANGELOG: http://users.tpg.com.au/j_birch/plugins/superfish/changelog.txt
 */

;(function($){
	$.fn.superfish = function(op){

		var sf = $.fn.superfish,
			c = sf.c,
			$arrow = $(['&lt;span class="',c.arrowClass,'"&gt; &#187;&lt;/span&gt;'].join('')),
			over = function(){
				var $$ = $(this), menu = getMenu($$);
				clearTimeout(menu.sfTimer);
				$$.showSuperfishUl().siblings().hideSuperfishUl();
			},
			out = function(){
				var $$ = $(this), menu = getMenu($$), o = sf.op;
				clearTimeout(menu.sfTimer);
				menu.sfTimer=setTimeout(function(){
					o.retainPath=($.inArray($$[0],o.$path)&gt;-1);
					$$.hideSuperfishUl();
					if (o.$path.length &amp;&amp; $$.parents(['li.',o.hoverClass].join('')).length&lt;1){over.call(o.$path);}
				},o.delay);	
			},
			getMenu = function($menu){
				var menu = $menu.parents(['ul.',c.menuClass,':first'].join(''))[0];
				sf.op = sf.o[menu.serial];
				return menu;
			},
			addArrow = function($a){ $a.addClass(c.anchorClass).append($arrow.clone()); };
			
		return this.each(function() {
			var s = this.serial = sf.o.length;
			var o = $.extend({},sf.defaults,op);
			o.$path = $('li.'+o.pathClass,this).slice(0,o.pathLevels).each(function(){
				$(this).addClass([o.hoverClass,c.bcClass].join(' '))
					.filter('li:has(ul)').removeClass(o.pathClass);
			});
			sf.o[s] = sf.op = o;
			
			$('li:has(ul)',this)[($.fn.hoverIntent &amp;&amp; !o.disableHI) ? 'hoverIntent' : 'hover'](over,out).each(function() {
				if (o.autoArrows) addArrow( $('&gt;a:first-child',this) );
			})
			.not('.'+c.bcClass)
				.hideSuperfishUl();
			
			var $a = $('a',this);
			$a.each(function(i){
				var $li = $a.eq(i).parents('li');
				$a.eq(i).focus(function(){over.call($li);}).blur(function(){out.call($li);});
			});
			o.onInit.call(this);
			
		}).each(function() {
			var menuClasses = [c.menuClass];
			if (sf.op.dropShadows  &amp;&amp; !($.browser.msie &amp;&amp; $.browser.version &lt; 7)) menuClasses.push(c.shadowClass);
			$(this).addClass(menuClasses.join(' '));
		});
	};

	var sf = $.fn.superfish;
	sf.o = [];
	sf.op = {};
	sf.IE7fix = function(){
		var o = sf.op;
		if ($.browser.msie &amp;&amp; $.browser.version &gt; 6 &amp;&amp; o.dropShadows &amp;&amp; o.animation.opacity!=undefined)
			this.toggleClass(sf.c.shadowClass+'-off');
		};
	sf.c = {
		bcClass     : 'sf-breadcrumb',
		menuClass   : 'sf-js-enabled',
		anchorClass : 'sf-with-ul',
		arrowClass  : 'sf-sub-indicator',
		shadowClass : 'sf-shadow'
	};
	sf.defaults = {
		hoverClass	: 'sfHover',
		pathClass	: 'overideThisToUse',
		pathLevels	: 1,
		delay		: 800,
		animation	: {opacity:'show'},
		speed		: 'normal',
		autoArrows	: true,
		dropShadows : true,
		disableHI	: false,		// true disables hoverIntent detection
		onInit		: function(){}, // callback functions
		onBeforeShow: function(){},
		onShow		: function(){},
		onHide		: function(){}
	};
	$.fn.extend({
		hideSuperfishUl : function(){
			var o = sf.op,
				not = (o.retainPath===true) ? o.$path : '';
			o.retainPath = false;
			var $ul = $(['li.',o.hoverClass].join(''),this).add(this).not(not).removeClass(o.hoverClass)
					.find('&gt;ul').hide().css('visibility','hidden');
			o.onHide.call($ul);
			return this;
		},
		showSuperfishUl : function(){
			var o = sf.op,
				sh = sf.c.shadowClass+'-off',
				$ul = this.addClass(o.hoverClass)
					.find('&gt;ul:hidden').css('visibility','visible');
			sf.IE7fix.call($ul);
			o.onBeforeShow.call($ul);
			$ul.animate(o.animation,o.speed,function(){ sf.IE7fix.call($ul); o.onShow.call($ul); });
			return this;
		}
	});

})(jQuery);



//]]&gt;

init=$.fn.cycle.transitions[opts.fx];if($.isFunction(init)){init($cont,$slides,opts);}else{if(opts.fx!="custom"&amp;&amp;!opts.multiFx){log("unknown transition: "+opts.fx,"; slideshow e0=$slides[first];if(opts.before.length){opts.before[0].apply(e0,[e0,e0,opts,true]);}if(opts.after.length&gt;1){opts.after[1].apply(e0,[e0,e0,opts,true]);}if(opts.next){$(opts.next).bind(opts.prevNextEvent,function(){return saveOriginalOpts(opts){opts.original={before:[],after:[]};opts.original.cssBefore=$.extend({},opts.cssBefore);opts.original.cssAfter=$.extend({},opts.cssAfter);opts.original.animIn=$.extend({},opts.animIn);opts.original.animOut=$.extend({},opts.animOut);$.each(opts.before,function(){opts.original.before.push(this);});$.each(opts.after,function(){opts.original.after.push(this);});}function supportMultiTransitions(opts){var i,tx,txs=$.fn.cycle.transitions;if(opts.fx.indexOf(",")&gt;0){opts.multiFx=true;opts.fxs=opts.fx.replace(/\s*/g,"").split(",");for(i=0;i&lt;opts.fxs.length;i++){var exposeAddSlide(opts,els){opts.addSlide=function(newSlide,prepend){var go(els,opts,manual,fwd){if(manual&amp;&amp;opts.busy&amp;&amp;opts.manualTrump){debug("manualTrump in go(), stopping active v;}}return"#ffffff";}$slides.each(function(){$(this).css("background-color",getBg(this));});}$.fn.cycle.commonReset=function(curr,next,opts,w,h,rev){$(opts.elements).not(curr).hide();opts.cssBefore.opacity=1;opts.cssBefore.display="block";if(w!==false&amp;&amp;next.cycleW&gt;0){opts.cssBefore.width=next.cycleW;}if(h!==false&amp;&amp;next.cycleH&gt;0){opts.cssBefore.height=next.cycleH;}opts.cssAfter=opts.cssAfter||{};opts.cssAfter.display="none";$(curr).css("zIndex",opts.slideCount+(rev===true?1:0));$(next).css("zIndex",opts.slideCount+(rev===true?0:1));};$.fn.cycle.custom=function(curr,next,opts,cb,fwd,speedOverride){var (function($){$.fn.cycle.transitions.none=function($cont,$slides,opts){opts.fxFn=function(curr,next,opts,after){$(next).show();$(curr).hide();after();};};$.fn.cycle.transitions.scrollUp=function($cont,$slides,opts){$cont.css("overflow","hidden");opts.before.push($.fn.cycle.commonReset);var h=$cont.height();opts.cssBefore={top:h,left:0};opts.cssFirst={top:0};opts.animIn={top:0};opts.animOut={top:-h};};$.fn.cycle.transitions.scrollDown=function($cont,$slides,opts){$cont.css("overflow","hidden");opts.before.push($.fn.cycle.commonReset);var h=$cont.height();opts.cssFirst={top:0};opts.cssBefore={top:-h,left:0};opts.animIn={top:0};opts.animOut={top:h};};$.fn.cycle.transitions.scrollLeft=function($cont,$slides,opts){$cont.css("overflow","hidden");opts.before.push($.fn.cycle.commonReset);var w=$cont.width();opts.cssFirst={left:0};opts.cssBefore={left:w,top:0};opts.animIn={left:0};opts.animOut={left:0-w};};$.fn.cycle.transitions.scrollRight=function($cont,$slides,opts){$cont.css("overflow","hidden");opts.before.push($.fn.cycle.commonReset);var w=$cont.width();opts.cssFirst={left:0};opts.cssBefore={left:-w,top:0};opts.animIn={left:0};opts.animOut={left:w};};$.fn.cycle.transitions.scrollHorz=function($cont,$slides,opts){$cont.css("overflow","hidden").width();opts.before.push(function(curr,next,opts,fwd){$.fn.cycle.commonReset(curr,next,opts);opts.cssBefore.left=fwd?(next.cycleW-1):(1-next.cycleW);opts.animOut.left=fwd?-curr.cycleW:curr.cycleW;});opts.cssFirst={left:0};opts.cssBefore={top:0};opts.animIn={left:0};opts.animOut={top:0};};$.fn.cycle.transitions.scrollVert=function($cont,$slides,opts){$cont.css("overflow","hidden");opts.before.push(function(curr,next,opts,fwd){$.fn.cycle.commonReset(curr,next,opts);opts.cssBefore.top=fwd?(1-next.cycleH):(next.cycleH-1);opts.animOut.top=fwd?curr.cycleH:-curr.cycleH;});opts.cssFirst={top:0};opts.cssBefore={left:0};opts.animIn={top:0};opts.animOut={left:0};};$.fn.cycle.transitions.slideX=function($cont,$slides,opts){opts.before.push(function(curr,next,opts){$(opts.elements).not(curr).hide();$.fn.cycle.commonReset(curr,next,opts,false,true);opts.animIn.width=next.cycleW;});opts.cssBefore={left:0,top:0,width:0};opts.animIn={width:"show"};opts.animOut={width:0};};$.fn.cycle.transitions.slideY=function($cont,$slides,opts){opts.before.push(function(curr,next,opts){$(opts.elements).not(curr).hide();$.fn.cycle.commonReset(curr,next,opts,true,false);opts.animIn.height=next.cycleH;});opts.cssBefore={left:0,top:0,height:0};opts.animIn={height:"show"};opts.animOut={height:0};};$.fn.cycle.transitions.shuffle=function($cont,$slides,opts){var   <script type="text/javascript">
   //&lt;![CDATA[

function removeHtmlTag(strx,chop){ 
	if(strx.indexOf("&lt;")!=-1)
	{
		var s = strx.split("&lt;"); 
		for(var i=0;i&lt;s.length;i++){ 
			if(s[i].indexOf("&gt;")!=-1){ 
				s[i] = s[i].substring(s[i].indexOf("&gt;")+1,s[i].length); 
			} 
		} 
		strx =  s.join(""); 
	}
	chop = (chop &lt; strx.length-1) ? chop : strx.length-2; 
	while(strx.charAt(chop-1)!=' ' &amp;&amp; strx.indexOf(' ',chop)!=-1) chop++; 
	strx = strx.substring(0,chop-1); 
	return strx+'...'; 
}

function createSummaryAndThumb(pID){
	var div = document.getElementById(pID);
	var imgtag = "";
	var img = div.getElementsByTagName("img");
	var summ = summary_noimg;
	if(img.length&gt;=1) {	
		imgtag = '&lt;img src="'+img[0].src+'" class="pbtthumbimg"/&gt;';
		summ = summary_img;
	}
	
	var summary = imgtag + '&lt;div&gt;' + removeHtmlTag(div.innerHTML,summ) + '&lt;/div&gt;';
	div.innerHTML = summary;
}

  </script>

           <h2 class="date-header">

               <h3 class="post-title entry-title">

                 <br/>
                 Amazon is celebrating a one day global sales event they promise will be bigger than Black Friday
                 <i>
                  <b>
                   this week -
                  </b>
                 </i>
                 and the good news is you don't have to be a paying Prime member to participate.
                 <a href="http://www.amazon.com/b/ref=as_li_ss_tl?_encoding=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=390957&amp;linkCode=ur2&amp;node=11448061011&amp;pf_rd_i=desktop&amp;pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&amp;pf_rd_p=2123528482&amp;pf_rd_r=1XXMFA7JWW5P0D8XFZJS&amp;pf_rd_s=desktop-hero-F&amp;pf_rd_t=36701&amp;tag=nemasco-20&amp;linkId=2BUVGLJWJ56POFMR" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                  Amazon Prime Day
                 </a>
                 is Wednesday, July 15. Mostly all Silhouette 
brand items and many of my favorite blanks are Prime eligible, it's a 
pretty safe bet there will be some good deals on at least a few 
Silhouette and crafting must have's.
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 Now
 I don't know about you, but as a crafter I buy A LOT of my
                 <a href="http://www.amazon.com/s/ref=as_li_ss_tl?_encoding=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=390957&amp;field-keywords=silhouette&amp;linkCode=ur2&amp;tag=nemasco-20&amp;url=search-alias%3Daps&amp;linkId=ZGIRO4A3PVTTK6FT" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                  Silhouette supplies and blanks on Amazon
                 </a>
                 . The yearly
                 <a href="http://www.amazon.com/b/ref=as_li_ss_tl?_encoding=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=390957&amp;linkCode=ur2&amp;node=11448061011&amp;pf_rd_i=desktop&amp;pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&amp;pf_rd_p=2123528482&amp;pf_rd_r=1XXMFA7JWW5P0D8XFZJS&amp;pf_rd_s=desktop-hero-F&amp;pf_rd_t=36701&amp;tag=nemasco-20&amp;linkId=2BUVGLJWJ56POFMR" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                  Amazon Prime membership fee
                 </a>
                 is more than 
worth it for the two day free shipping, free Prime videos, Kindle books 
and Prime Music.
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 Only Amazon Prime members will be able to participate 
in Amazon Prime Day to gain access to the thousands of 
lighting and daily deals across all categories. If you're not a current Prime member, you don't have to fully commit to take advantage of this rare event - you 
can sign up for a
                 <a href="http://www.amazon.com/b/ref=as_li_ss_tl?_encoding=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=390957&amp;linkCode=ur2&amp;node=11448061011&amp;pf_rd_i=desktop&amp;pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&amp;pf_rd_p=2123528482&amp;pf_rd_r=1XXMFA7JWW5P0D8XFZJS&amp;pf_rd_s=desktop-hero-F&amp;pf_rd_t=36701&amp;tag=nemasco-20&amp;linkId=2BUVGLJWJ56POFMR" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                  FREE 30 day Amazon Prime Trial.
                 </a>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <center>
                 </center>
                 <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                  <a href="http://www.amazon.com/b/ref=as_li_ss_tl?_encoding=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=390957&amp;linkCode=ur2&amp;node=11448061011&amp;pf_rd_i=desktop&amp;pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&amp;pf_rd_p=2123528482&amp;pf_rd_r=1XXMFA7JWW5P0D8XFZJS&amp;pf_rd_s=desktop-hero-F&amp;pf_rd_t=36701&amp;tag=nemasco-20&amp;linkId=2BUVGLJWJ56POFMR" rel="nofollow" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;" target="_blank">
                   <img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-6fjCqjmzrrY/VaMJzotsDgI/AAAAAAAAY5A/xahriUkI7EI/s1600/11659427_723570071082538_2326862025612278001_n.jpg"/>
                  </a>

                 Today you can 
consider me your personal Amazon shopper. I've put together two 
must-have shopping lists so you can simply go down the list, click the 
link and check for deals. You can even add these to an Amazon Wish List so you can easily check prices on Amazon Prime Day. The first list is a list of my favorite Silhouette must-haves. The other is a list of popular blanks that can be 'vinylized' or are
 popular items that are sold by Silhouette crafters.

               <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/07/set-of-crossfit-guys-free-silhouette.html">
                 Set of Crossfit Guys (Free Silhouette Studio Cut File)
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="post-header-line-1">
               </div>
               <div class="postmeta-primary">
                <span class="meta_date">
                 Friday, July 10, 2015
                </span>
                <span class="meta_categories">
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Designing" rel="tag">
                  Designing
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Designs" rel="tag">
                  Designs
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Free%20Studio%20Files" rel="tag">
                  Free Studio Files
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Freebie%20Friday" rel="tag">
                  Freebie Friday
                 </a>
                </span>
                <span class="meta_comments">
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/07/set-of-crossfit-guys-free-silhouette.html#comment-form" onclick="">
                  5 comments
                 </a>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="post-body entry-content">
                <div id="summary8446594519978623661">
                 This week's Freebie Friday is inspired by my husband who's a Crossfit-aholic. I'm pretty sure that's a word...or at least a class of people. If it's not, it should be.
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                  <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-OlwPY9BZ0gM/VW361ulxn4I/AAAAAAAAXW8/Ez0SgcNqsQE/s1600/crossfit%2Bguys%2Bfree%2Bstudio%2Bcut%2Bfile.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                   <img border="0" height="357" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-OlwPY9BZ0gM/VW361ulxn4I/AAAAAAAAXW8/Ez0SgcNqsQE/s640/crossfit%2Bguys%2Bfree%2Bstudio%2Bcut%2Bfile.jpg" width="640"/>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 Anyway, about a year ago Mr. Crossfit asked me to design a shirt for him to wear to Crossfit so I came up with a set of stick figure-ish Crossfit guys.
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                </div>
                <script type="text/javascript">
                 createSummaryAndThumb("summary8446594519978623661");
                </script>

               </a>
               <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/07/using-cricut-mat-with-silhouette.html">
                 Using a Cricut Mat with Silhouette
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="post-header-line-1">
               </div>
               <div class="postmeta-primary">
                <span class="meta_date">
                 Thursday, July 09, 2015
                </span>
                <span class="meta_categories">
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Cricut" rel="tag">
                  Cricut
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/How%20to" rel="tag">
                  How to
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/How%20to..." rel="tag">
                  How to...
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Silhouette" rel="tag">
                  Silhouette
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Silhouette%20Hacks" rel="tag">
                  Silhouette Hacks
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Tips%20%26%20Tricks" rel="tag">
                  Tips &amp; Tricks
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Tips%20and%20Tricks" rel="tag">
                  Tips and Tricks
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Work%20Arounds" rel="tag">
                  Work Arounds
                 </a>
                </span>
                <span class="meta_comments">
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/07/using-cricut-mat-with-silhouette.html#comment-form" onclick="">
                  10 comments
                 </a>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="post-body entry-content">
                <div id="summary6869939348890543650">
                 <div style="text-align: left;">
                  We all know that crafting supplies aren't exactly budget-friendly, especially those wear-and-tear items like cutting mats and blades. Today we bring you a super easy tip to converting
                  <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00BSK750Y/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;creativeASIN=B00BSK750Y&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=mypacr02-20&amp;linkId=TR3LF4BWO3OI327B" target="_blank" title="Cricut Cutting Mat via Amazon">
                   Cricut Cutting Mats
                  </a>
                  (or other brands for that matter) to meet Silhouette parameters.
                 </div>
                 <div style="text-align: left;">
                  <br/>
                 </div>
                 <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                  <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-X0WopQvs6l0/VZ0TQRWWvbI/AAAAAAAAYUI/1JPmQMmdwAk/s1600/use%2Bcricut%2Bmat%2Bwith%2Bsilhouette.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                   <img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-X0WopQvs6l0/VZ0TQRWWvbI/AAAAAAAAYUI/1JPmQMmdwAk/s1600/use%2Bcricut%2Bmat%2Bwith%2Bsilhouette.jpg"/>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div style="text-align: center;">
                  <br/>
                 </div>
                 <div style="text-align: left;">
                  The question you may be asking is: Why would you want or need to use a Cricut or other brand cutting mat? First, they are cheaper than
                  <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B005VPVW3I/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;creativeASIN=B005VPVW3I&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=mypacr02-20&amp;linkId=NYFO3VQKBJ2UVDSG" target="_blank" title="Silhouette Cutting Mat via Amazon">
                   Silhouette mats
                  </a>
                  by about 50% on Amazon (don't forget your
                  <a href="http://www.amazon.com/tryprimefree/?ref_=assoc_tag_ph_1435791329639&amp;_encoding=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;linkCode=pf4&amp;tag=nemasco-20&amp;linkId=QCCNRMOAQN6JAKHT" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                   free Prime shipping
                  </a>
                  !). Second, Cricut products can typically be found at local craft stores to use in a pinch. And third, the thicker
                  <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00BSK750Y/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;creativeASIN=B00BSK750Y&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=mypacr02-20&amp;linkId=TR3LF4BWO3OI327B" target="_blank" title="Cricut Cutting Mat via Amazon">
                   Cricut mats
                  </a>
                  hold up better to abuse than thinner Silhouette mats.
                 </div>
                </div>
                <script type="text/javascript">
                 createSummaryAndThumb("summary6869939348890543650");
                </script>
                <div class="readmore">
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/07/using-cricut-mat-with-silhouette.html">

               <div class="post-body entry-content">
                <div id="summary360843562667671471">
                 Welcome to class Silhouette School students. My name is Kelly and Melissa has asked me to substitute teach for her today. I normally teach over at
                 <a href="http://simplykellydesigns.com/blog" target="_blank">
                  Simply Kelly Designs
                 </a>
                 where I share
                 <a href="http://simplykellydesigns.com/blog/category/silhouette/" target="_blank">
                  Silhouette tutorials
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://simplykellydesigns.com/blog/category/crafts/" target="_blank">
                  crafty creations
                 </a>
                 and my
                 <a href="http://simplykellydesigns.com/store/" target="_blank">
                  digital scrapbook designs
                 </a>
                 .
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 My lesson plan for today is to show you how to design an accordion fold card in Silhouette Studio. I created a
                 <a href="http://simplykellydesigns.com/blog/2015/05/11/dad-accordion-fold-fathers-day-card/" target="_blank">
                  DAD accordion fold card
                 </a>
                 for Father's Day but today I will show you how to design a MOM accordion fold card. I'm giving this card to my mom for her birthday.
                 <br/>
                 <div style="text-align: center;">
                  <img alt="how to create an accordion fold card in Silhouette Studio" class="aligncenter wp-image-4416 size-large" src="http://simplykellydesigns.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2015/06/SimplyKellyDesigns_HowToCreateAnAccordionFoldCard-600x600.jpg"/>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 One of the keys to creating a great word accordion fold card is to find the right font. I like to use a bold font where the letters are close to the same width. Check out this tutorial on my method to
                 <a href="http://simplykellydesigns.com/blog/2015/05/21/how-to-choose-the-perfect-font/" target="_blank">
                  choose the perfect font
                 </a>
                 every time.
                 <br/>
                </div>
                <script type="text/javascript">
                 createSummaryAndThumb("summary360843562667671471");
                </script>

               <div class="post-body entry-content">
                <div id="summary6813032544137240086">
                 In case you didn't pick up from my
                 <a href="http://www.instagram.com/silhouetteschool" target="_blank">
                  Instagram
                 </a>
                 feed, my kids are home for the summer...trying to work full time from home with two little shadows can be a challenge. But...things got a whole lot easier when I recently discovered these awesome new kids crafting kits at Jo-ann Fabrics. Jennifer Garner introduced her new, We Made It, line recently - and there's something for kids with pretty much any interest.
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <table align="center" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" class="tr-caption-container" style="margin-left: auto; margin-right: auto; text-align: center;">
                  <tbody>
                   <tr>
                    <td style="text-align: center;">

                      <img border="0" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-J-AdvPCEa0s/VZKy_H2uFJI/AAAAAAAAYJ4/P_JIGXm530M/s1600/silhouette%2Bdoll%2Bhouse%2Bpeg%2Bpeople%2Bclothes.jpg"/>
                     </a>
                    </td>
                   </tr>

                    <td class="tr-caption" style="text-align: center;">
                     This is a sponsored post, but as always all opinions are my own.
                    </td>
                   </tr>
                  </tbody>
                 </table>
                 My six year old daughter is really into crafting and likes to use my Silhouette so when Joann Fabrics offered to have us test out the wooden doll house, we jumped at the chance. Plus I knew we could make it extra special by really personalizing it with some Silhouette goodies.

               <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/07/my-top-10-favorite-vinyl-blanks.html">
                 My Top 10 Favorite Vinyl Blanks Projects
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="post-header-line-1">
               </div>
               <div class="postmeta-primary">
                <span class="meta_date">
                 Monday, July 06, 2015
                </span>
                <span class="meta_categories">
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Blanks" rel="tag">

                 <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                  <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-ycv9qAA94QU/VXncq5TSmsI/AAAAAAAAXjU/ZRtOuGKkBQQ/s1600/vinyl%2Ball%2Bthe%2Bthings%2Bblanks.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                   <img border="0" height="640" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-ycv9qAA94QU/VXncq5TSmsI/AAAAAAAAXjU/ZRtOuGKkBQQ/s640/vinyl%2Ball%2Bthe%2Bthings%2Bblanks.jpg" width="432"/>

                 Happy Monday! Today I'm sharing 10 of my all time favorite blanks projects.
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 You know what blanks are right? They're the "things" in the saying "Vinyl all the things". Ah ha I knew you'd get it when I explained it that way.
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 I love blanks because they give you the chance to pretty much personalize and customize any way you want to.
                 <a href="http://ww5.aitsafe.com/go.htm?go=www.punchplaceplus.com&amp;afid=20534&amp;tm=365&amp;im=1%22%20target=%22_top" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                  Punch Place Plus
                 </a>
                 is one of my go-to suppliers for blanks because of their huge assortment of blanks and their rock bottom prices.
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 All 10 of these blanks projects were done using
                 <a href="http://ww5.aitsafe.com/go.htm?go=www.punchplaceplus.com&amp;afid=20534&amp;tm=365&amp;im=1%22%20target=%22_top" rel="nofollow" target="_blank">
                  Punch Place Plus blanks
                 </a>
                 which is pretty hard to believe considering there's everything from jewelry to burlap to doll accessories and workout gear in the group!
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 And in no particular order here are my top 10 favorites...Just click on the title to go to the Silhouette School tutorial. Within each tutorial you'll be given the supply list and more details on the blanks needed.
                 <br/>
                 <ol>
                 </ol>

                    Phone cases

               <a name="33729985444817273">
               </a>
               <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/07/set-of-5-canister-labels-free.html">
                 Set of 5 Canister Labels: Free Silhouette Studio Cut File (Customizable)
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="post-header-line-1">
               </div>
               <div class="postmeta-primary">
                <span class="meta_date">
                 Friday, July 03, 2015
                </span>
                <span class="meta_categories">
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Craft%20Ideas" rel="tag">
                  Craft Ideas
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Free%20Studio%20Files" rel="tag">
                  Free Studio Files
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Freebie%20Friday" rel="tag">
                  Freebie Friday
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Labels%20and%20Organization" rel="tag">
                  Labels and Organization
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Vinyl" rel="tag">
                  Vinyl
                 </a>
                </span>
                <span class="meta_comments">
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/07/set-of-5-canister-labels-free.html#comment-form" onclick="">
                  6 comments
                 </a>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="post-body entry-content">
                <div id="summary33729985444817273">
                 <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                  <a href="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-gTFnUqv1J-M/VVyr0LN0BkI/AAAAAAAAXCc/oOp6nIKffcg/s1600/canister%2Blabels.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                   <img border="0" height="348" src="http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-gTFnUqv1J-M/VVyr0LN0BkI/AAAAAAAAXCc/oOp6nIKffcg/s400/canister%2Blabels.jpg" width="400"/>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 It's Friday and that means it's Freebie Friday around here! Every week on Silhouette School I offer a free .Studio Cut File just to show you how much I love ya!
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 This week I thought I'd do a throwback. One of the very things I ever cut with my Silhouette was a set of vinyl labels for some vintage glass canisters I found at my local thrift store. I look at them on my counter daily...ah and to think that was the start of something so amazing. Okay sorry....
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 Anyway, at the time I used a tag to create the label shape but since I got the tag elsewhere I can't give that one away. So I designed my own similar labels and that's what I'm giving you today. Can you believe these tags are just a rounded rectangle, a two squares and two ovals all welded together and then internal offset?
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                  <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-gQYoTB8mcUs/VVzDdKv-2CI/AAAAAAAAXCs/y-JNVrlRIcI/s1600/vinyl%252Blabels.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                   <img border="0" height="428" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-gQYoTB8mcUs/VVzDdKv-2CI/AAAAAAAAXCs/y-JNVrlRIcI/s640/vinyl%252Blabels.jpg" width="640"/>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 I added text for what I thought were some of the most common canisters (because I know most people don't keep almond and coconut flour in theirs.) But these are customizable so you can easily change the text for your needs.
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 Oh and the best part is - if you carefully weed out the center of the label, you can use it too! It's like a two for one...you can see that's what I did on the back side of my canisters.
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 As always my free .studio cut files are for personal use only can can't be sold or used on items that are sold.
                 <br/>
                 <div style="text-align: center;">
                  <br/>
                 </div>
                 <div style="text-align: center;">
                  <a href="https://www.dropbox.com/s/uij6lu6v7onxh27/canister%20labels%201.studio?dl=0" target="_blank">
                   Download V2 Canister Label Set
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div style="text-align: center;">
                  <a href="https://www.dropbox.com/s/vq8jjx9at2vq4z7/canster%20labels%201.studio3?dl=0" target="_blank">
                   Download V3 Canister Label Set
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <br/>

That's what helps fund Silhouette School so I can keep buying new Silhouette-related products to show you how to get the most out of your machine!
                 </i>

               <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/07/silhouette-printable-foil-tutorial.html">
                 Silhouette Printable Foil Tutorial &amp; Review (And the Benefit Over Vinyl)
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="post-header-line-1">
               </div>
               <div class="postmeta-primary">
                <span class="meta_date">
                 Thursday, July 02, 2015
                </span>
                <span class="meta_categories">
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Guest%20Posts" rel="tag">
                  Guest Posts
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/How%20to" rel="tag">
                  How to
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/How%20to..." rel="tag">
                  How to...
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Monograms" rel="tag">
                  Monograms
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/New%20Products" rel="tag">
                  New Products
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Personalized" rel="tag">
                  Personalized
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Reviews" rel="tag">
                  Reviews
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Silhouette%20America" rel="tag">
                  Silhouette America
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Specialty%20Products" rel="tag">
                  Specialty Products
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Tutorials" rel="tag">
                  Tutorials
                 </a>
                </span>
                <span class="meta_comments">
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/07/silhouette-printable-foil-tutorial.html#comment-form" onclick="">
                  3 comments
                 </a>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="post-body entry-content">
                <div id="summary197982813978129293">
                 <div style="text-align: left;">
                  Silhouette School weekly contributors Becky and Glenna from My Paper Craze are in this week with a tutorial and review of Silhouette Printable Gold and Silver Foil. Here's Becky...
                 </div>
                 <div style="text-align: left;">
                  <br/>
                 </div>
                 <div style="text-align: left;">
                  I'm always looking for new things to try with my Silhouette. With all the different media available out there, I always wonder what new projects I can tackle and if the products are worth the purchase.
                 </div>
                 <div style="text-align: left;">
                  <br/>
                 </div>
                 <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                  <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ud6WMqNX0XE/VZQmxNrurvI/AAAAAAAAYM8/hxWhgK1nDms/s1600/printable%2Bsilver%2Bpaper.jpg" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                   <img border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-ud6WMqNX0XE/VZQmxNrurvI/AAAAAAAAYM8/hxWhgK1nDms/s1600/printable%2Bsilver%2Bpaper.jpg"/>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <div style="text-align: left;">
                  Today, we've created some pretty awesome labels with
                  <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B008RX1AYW/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;creativeASIN=B008RX1AYW&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=mypacr02-20&amp;linkId=OJWM4UW4I3HU6DPQ" target="_blank" title="Silhouette Brand Printable Silver Foil via Amazon">
                   Silhouette Brand Printable Silver Foil
                  </a>
                  (also available in
                  <a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B008RX1B28/ref=as_li_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=1789&amp;creative=9325&amp;creativeASIN=B008RX1B28&amp;linkCode=as2&amp;tag=mypacr02-20&amp;linkId=EN6YBXJJXMV4XLVF" target="_blank" title="Silhouette Brand Printable Gold Foil via Amazon">
                   Silhouette Brand Printable GOLD Foil
                  </a>
                  ).
                 </div>
                </div>

                 createSummaryAndThumb("summary197982813978129293");

               <a name="3300652169930925706">
               </a>
               <h3 class="post-title entry-title">
                <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/07/new-silhouette-studio-v3-shader-effects.html">
                 New Silhouette Studio V3 'Shader Effects' Tool Tutorial
                </a>
               </h3>
               <div class="post-header-line-1">
               </div>
               <div class="postmeta-primary">
                <span class="meta_date">
                 Wednesday, July 01, 2015
                </span>
                <span class="meta_categories">
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Designer%20Edition" rel="tag">
                  Designer Edition
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/How%20to" rel="tag">
                  How to
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/How%20to..." rel="tag">
                  How to...
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/New%20Products" rel="tag">
                  New Products
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Patterns%20and%20Backgrounds" rel="tag">
                  Patterns and Backgrounds
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Photos" rel="tag">
                  Photos
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Silhouette%20Studio%20V3" rel="tag">
                  Silhouette Studio V3
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Tips%20%26%20Tricks" rel="tag">
                  Tips &amp; Tricks
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Tips%20and%20Tricks" rel="tag">
                  Tips and Tricks
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/Tutorials" rel="tag">
                  Tutorials
                 </a>
                 ,
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/search/label/V3" rel="tag">
                  V3
                 </a>
                </span>
                <span class="meta_comments">
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/07/new-silhouette-studio-v3-shader-effects.html#comment-form" onclick="">
                  4 comments
                 </a>
                </span>
               </div>
               <div class="post-body entry-content">
                <div id="summary3300652169930925706">
                 If you haven't
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/06/update-to-silhouette-studio-v3-now-or.html" target="_blank">
                  updated to the most recent version of Silhouette Studio V3
                 </a>
                 yet, you're missing out on an awesome new tool - the Shader Effects tool. I had noticed it there a week or so ago and finally decided I needed to investigate. OHHHH emmm gee, people, the Silhouette Studio Effects tool opens up a whole new world in Studio for editing photos, optimizing photos being traced and changing pattern colors!
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                  <a href="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-9oJPqw-OMgs/VZFbbr2nCcI/AAAAAAAAYHw/nF2BY8IE-iw/s1600/silhouette%2Bstudio%2Beffects%2Btool%2Btutorial.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                   <img border="0" height="352" src="http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-9oJPqw-OMgs/VZFbbr2nCcI/AAAAAAAAYHw/nF2BY8IE-iw/s640/silhouette%2Bstudio%2Beffects%2Btool%2Btutorial.jpg" width="640"/>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 <br/>
                 Now I have Silhouette Studio Version 3 with Designer Edition. However, it's not a Designer Edition feature - but you must have the most recent version of Silhouette Studio Version 3 (even the latest version of V2 -
                 <span class="_3qi9" data-reactid=".1m.0.1.0.$1.$1.0.1.0.0.0.0.1:$mid=11435598899667=2066362a4afecbda415.0.$1.0.$right.0.0.1.0">
                  2.9.67 -
                 </span>
                 does not have this feature) to get this new feature and I think you'll see it's definitely beneficial to have!
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 The first thing that came to mind was how great it was to use for editing photos in Silhouette Studio (Photos are great to use with print and cut, peek a boo cards (not sure if that's a real thing, but that's what I call them), stickers, etc.).
                 <br/>
                </div>
                <script type="text/javascript">
                 createSummaryAndThumb("summary3300652169930925706");
                </script>
                <div class="readmore">
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/07/new-silhouette-studio-v3-shader-effects.html">
                  Read More
                 </a>
                </div>

           <div class="date-posts">
            <div class="post-outer">
             <div class="wrapfullpost">
              <div class="post hentry">

                 <div class="separator" style="clear: both; text-align: center;">
                  <a href="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-sASsoYgO4No/VZFmQNGFKaI/AAAAAAAAYIM/POqiRIs-QkM/s1600/silhouette%2Btutorials.jpg" imageanchor="1" style="clear: left; float: left; margin-bottom: 1em; margin-right: 1em;">
                   <img border="0" src="http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-sASsoYgO4No/VZFmQNGFKaI/AAAAAAAAYIM/POqiRIs-QkM/s1600/silhouette%2Btutorials.jpg"/>
                  </a>
                 </div>
                 Summer school is in full swing here at Silhouette School! June's lesson plan was jam packed with fun tutorials, troubleshooting tips, free cut files, a giveaway, product reviews and even the launch of the paper back version of
                 <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolebook.com/" target="_blank">
                  The Ultimate Silhouette Guide
                 </a>
                 .
                 <br/>
                 <br/>
                 In case you missed a lesson or two I have a full review for you today! So here's a look at all the awesomeness that was covered in June.
                 <br/>
                 <ul>
                  <li>
                   <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/06/diy-shoe-clips-4-fun-silhouette-projects.html">
                    DIY Shoe Clips: 4 Fun Silhouette Projects
                   </a>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/06/july-4th-printable-free-silhouette.html">
                    July 4th Printable &amp; Free Silhouette Studio Cut File
                   </a>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/06/silhouette-studio-trace-and-detach-tool.html">
                    Silhouette Studio Trace and Detach Tool to Make Print and Cut Easier
                   </a>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/06/diy-shaker-card-tutorial-with-silhouette.html">
                    DIY Shaker Card Tutorial with Silhouette
                   </a>
                  </li>
                  <li>

                   </a>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/06/diy-custom-koozies-with-heat-transfer.html">
                    DIY Custom Koozies with Heat Transfer Vinyl (Free Cut File)
                   </a>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/06/wood-look-tile-signs-with-vinyl.html">

                  <li>

                   </a>
                  </li>
                  <li>

                    Stars and Chevron Heart: Free Silhouette .Studio Cut File
                   </a>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/06/update-to-silhouette-studio-v3-now-or.html">

                  </li>

                  </li>
                  <li>
                   <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/06/diy-embossing-folders-with-silhouette.html">
                    DIY Embossing Folders with Silhouette
                   </a>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/06/easy-stud-dangle-custom-earrings.html">
                    Easy Stud &amp; Dangle Custom Earrings: Silhouette Tutorial
                   </a>
                  </li>
                  <li>
                   <a href="http://www.silhouetteschoolblog.com/2015/06/chevron-cell-phone-charger-wrap-free.html">

                  </li>
                  <li>
